      "source": [
        "##Calculating Feature Importances"
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "markdown",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "pMmn729VgVUY"
      },
      "source": [
        "# To decide the pricing for various upcoming clothes, they wish to find how the style, season, and material affect the sales of a dress and if the style of the dress is more influential than its price.\n",
        "# Also, to increase sales, the management wants to analyze the attributes of dresses and find which are the leading factors affecting the sale of a dress.\n",
        "# To regularize the rating procedure and find its efficiency, the store wants to find if the rating of the dress affects the total sales"
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "metadata": {
        "colab": {
          "base_uri": "https://localhost:8080/",
          "height": 729
        },
        "id": "LwAnB0xitahq",
        "outputId": "361f8ea1-e912-43cd-b64a-c1f515b1c107"
      },
      "source": [
        "features = ad.columns\n",
        "importances = model.feature_importances_\n",
        "indices = (np.argsort(importances))[-100:]\n",
        "plt.figure(figsize=(10,12))\n",
